<div id="mobileSuggestOverlay" class="mobile-overlay-suggest"></div>
<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const searchInput = document.querySelector(".mobile-search-input");
  const suggestionsBox = document.querySelector(".mobile-suggestions");
  const overlay = document.getElementById("mobileSuggestOverlay");

  // ููุช ููฺฉูุณ ุฑู input ุจุงุดูุ ูพุดููุงุฏูุง ุธุงูุฑ ุจุดู
  searchInput.addEventListener("focus", () => {
    suggestionsBox.classList.add("active");
    overlay.classList.add("active");
  });

  // ููุช ฺฉูฺฉ ุจุฑูู ุงุฒ ุจุงฺฉุณ ุดุฏุ ุจุณุชู ุจุดู
  overlay.addEventListener("click", () => {
    suggestionsBox.classList.remove("active");
    overlay.classList.remove("active");
  });

  // ุงฺฏุฑ ุจุฎูุง ุจุง ุฏฺฉูู ุง ุขฺฉูู ุฎุงุต ุจุงุฒ ุจุดูุ ูโุชูู ุงูู ุงุถุงูู ฺฉู:
